                <div class="field-item">
                 <section about="" class="entity entity-paragraphs-item paragraphs-item-three-column band pad-none no-gutter clearfix" typeof="">
                  <section class="content band-content wrapper parts-span-third">
                   <div class="group-left field-group-div">
                    <div class="field field-name-field-left-block field-type-blockreference field-label-hidden">
                     <div class="field-items">
                      <div class="field-item">
                       <div class="block block-bean" id="block-bean-nc-opioid-overdose-deaths-drop-f">
                        <div class="content">
                         <div>
                          <div class="cards">
                           <div class="card article framed" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
                            <a href="/news/press-releases/food-and-nutrition-services-recipients-receive-temporary-15-increase-benefits" itemprop="url">
                             <span itemprop="photo">
                              <img alt="Food" height="376" src="https://files.nc.gov/ncdhhs/styles/card_photo/public/food_0.jpg?itok=1sdzNjXz" typeof="foaf:Image" width="500"/>
                             </span>
                             <div class="meta">
                              <h3 itemprop="name">
                               Food and Nutrition Services Recipients to Receive Temporary 15% Increase in Benefits.
                              </h3>
                              <p itemprop="description">
                               NCDHHS announced that Food and Nutrition Services recipients will see a temporary increase in the amount of benefits they receive. This increase is part of the federal Emergency Coronavirus Relief Act of 2020. "We know that COVID has created additional hardships and increased food insecurity for children and families,” said David Locklear, Deputy Director for Economic and Family Services. “We want to do everything possible to support North Carolinians who need help buying food and increasing benefits for hundreds of thousands of families will be instrumental in meeting that need." The maximum benefit amount for households receiving FNS will increase by 15% until June 30, 2021. This increase will end on June 30, 2021, when benefit amounts will return to their current levels.
                              </p>
                             </div>
                            </a>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                   <div class="group-middle field-group-div">
                    <div class="field field-name-field-middle-block field-type-blockreference field-label-hidden">
                     <div class="field-items">
                      <div class="field-item">
                       <div class="block block-bean" id="block-bean-ncdhhs-dedicates-new-broughton-h">
                        <div class="content">
                         <div>
                          <div class="cards">
                           <div class="card article framed" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
                            <a href="https://ncmedicaidplans.gov/" itemprop="url">
                             <span itemprop="photo">
                              <img alt="Adult holding child." height="376" src="https://files.nc.gov/ncdhhs/styles/card_photo/public/Medicaid-words-500x376.jpg?itok=siMjbk3G" typeof="foaf:Image" width="500"/>
                             </span>
                             <div class="meta">
                              <h3 itemprop="name">
                               Medicaid beneficiaries can now select the  health plan and primary care provider that is best for their family’s care.
                              </h3>
                              <p itemprop="description">
                               NCDHHS announced the official 
launch of open enrollment for NC 
Medicaid Managed Care which runs 
through May 14, 2021. Beneficiaries can 
enroll online, by calling the NC Medicaid 
Managed Care Call Center at 833-870-5500
(TTY: 833-870-5588) or through the free 
NC Medicaid Managed Care mobile app 
available on Google Play or the App Store.
They can also use the mail-in forms sent 
to them in the enrollment packet. 

Until Medicaid Managed Care begins on
July 1, 2021, beneficiaries will keep
receiving Medicaid and NC Health Choice
care and services the way they do now.
                              </p>
                             </div>
                            </a>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                         </div>

                <div class="field-item">
                 <section about="" class="entity entity-paragraphs-item paragraphs-item-two-column band theme-core-blue no-gutter clearfix" typeof="">
                  <header class="band-header wrapper">
                   <h2 class="section-title">
                    What We Do
                   </h2>
                  </header>
                  <section class="content band-content wrapper parts-span-two-third">
                   <div class="group-left field-group-div">
                    <div class="field field-name-field-left-markup field-type-text-long field-label-hidden">
                     <div class="field-items">
                      <div class="field-item">
                       <p>
                        The Department of Health and Human Services manages the delivery of health- and human-related services for all North Carolinians, especially our most vulnerable citizens – children, elderly, disabled and low-income families. The Department works closely with health care professionals, community leaders and advocacy groups; local, state and federal entities; and many other stakeholders to make this happen.
                       </p>
                       <p>
                        <a class="button ghost inverted" href="/about/overview">
                         Learn More About the Department
                        </a>
                       </p>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                   </div>

                <div class="field-item">
                 <section about="" class="entity entity-paragraphs-item paragraphs-item-two-column band pad-top no-gutter clearfix" typeof="">
                  <section class="content band-content wrapper parts-span-two-third">
                   <div class="group-left field-group-div">
                    <div class="field field-name-field-left-markup field-type-text-long field-label-hidden">
                     <div class="field-items">
                      <div class="field-item">
                       <h2>
                        Local Social Services Office
                       </h2>
                       <p>
                        Each county in North Carolina has a local social services agency available to answer questions. They should also be your first call if you suspect a child is being abused or neglected. We're here to help you find contact information for your local county office.
                       </p>
                       <p>
                        <a class="button ghost" href="/divisions/social-services/local-dss-directory">
                         Local County Offices
                        </a>
                       </p>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </section>
                 </section>
                </div>
               </div>
